#### 7.2.5 组件测试策略

| 测试类型 | 工具                              | 覆盖目标    | 说明                   |
| -------- | --------------------------------- | ----------- | ---------------------- |
| 单元测试 | Vitest + React Testing Library    | 所有组件    | 渲染、交互、状态变化   |
| 视觉回归 | Chromatic / Storybook Test Runner | 所有stories | 像素级对比，防止UI漂移 |
| 可访问性 | axe-core + Storybook a11y addon   | 所有组件    | 自动ARIA/对比度检查    |
| 交互测试 | Storybook Interactions            | 复杂组件    | 用户流程模拟           |
| 性能测试 | Lighthouse CI                     | 关键页面    | 首屏加载、CLS、LCP     |

### 7.3 数据库Migration基线脚本

#### 7.3.1 迁移工具选型

| 数据库     | 工具             | 版本  | 理由                         |
| ---------- | ---------------- | ----- | ---------------------------- |
| PostgreSQL | golang-migrate   | 4.17+ | Go生态，CLI+Go API，支持多源 |
| Milvus     | 自定义Python脚本 | -     | Milvus无原生迁移工具，需自建 |
| Neo4j      | neo4j-migrations | 2.9+  | Java生态，支持Cypher迁移     |
| Redis      | 无需迁移         | -     | 缓存数据，重建即可           |

#### 7.3.2 PostgreSQL迁移目录结构

```
/taichu-api/migrations/
├── README.md
├── Makefile
├── 000001_create_schemas.down.sql
├── 000001_create_schemas.up.sql
├── 000002_create_users_table.down.sql
├── 000002_create_users_table.up.sql
├── 000003_create_companies_table.down.sql
├── 000003_create_companies_table.up.sql
├── 000004_create_payment_tables.down.sql
├── 000004_create_payment_tables.up.sql
├── 000005_create_ai_knowledge_tables.down.sql
├── 000005_create_ai_knowledge_tables.up.sql
├── 000006_create_audit_tables.down.sql
├── 000006_create_audit_tables.up.sql
├── 000007_seed_tax_rates.down.sql
├── 000007_seed_tax_rates.up.sql
├── 000008_add_indexes.down.sql
├── 000008_add_indexes.up.sql
└── seed/
    ├── tax_rates.csv          # 税率种子数据
    ├── countries.csv          # 国家种子数据
    └── sanctions_ofac.csv     # OFAC制裁名单
```

#### 7.3.3 迁移脚本示例

```sql
-- 000001_create_schemas.up.sql
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS user;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS company;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS payment;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS ai;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS legal;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS audit;

-- 000002_create_users_table.up.sql
CREATE TABLE user.users (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    phone VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    real_name VARCHAR(100),
    id_type VARCHAR(20) CHECK (id_type IN ('passport', 'id_card', 'hk_id')),
    id_number VARCHAR(50),
    id_front_url VARCHAR(500),
    id_back_url VARCHAR(500),
    kyc_status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending'
        CHECK (kyc_status IN ('pending', 'reviewing', 'approved', 'rejected')),
    kyc_rejected_reason TEXT,
    dlc_level INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 1 CHECK (dlc_level BETWEEN 1 AND 9),
    dvc_balance DECIMAL(20, 8) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'active'
        CHECK (status IN ('active', 'suspended', 'deleted')),
    last_login_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    deleted_at TIMESTAMPTZ,

    CONSTRAINT uk_users_phone UNIQUE (phone),
    CONSTRAINT uk_users_email UNIQUE (email),
    CONSTRAINT uk_users_id_number UNIQUE (id_number)
);

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION user.tr_update_updated_at()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    NEW.updated_at = NOW();
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

CREATE TRIGGER tr_update_user_updated_at
    BEFORE UPDATE ON user.users
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE FUNCTION user.tr_update_updated_at();

CREATE VIEW user.active_users AS
SELECT * FROM user.users WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;

-- 000007_seed_tax_rates.up.sql
INSERT INTO ai.tax_rates (country, tax_type, rate, effective_date, source_url, verified) VALUES
('CN', 'CIT', 25.00, '2026-01-01', 'https://www.chinatax.gov.cn', true),
('CN-HI', 'CIT', 15.00, '2026-01-01', 'https://hainan.gov.cn', true),
('WS', 'CIT', 0.00, 'permanent', 'https://www.samoaic.gov.ws', true),
('HK', 'CIT', 16.50, '2026-01-01', 'https://www.ird.gov.hk', true),
('SG', 'CIT', 17.00, '2026-01-01', 'https://www.iras.gov.sg', true),
('TH', 'VAT', 7.00, '2026-01-01', 'https://www.rd.go.th', true),
('DE', 'VAT', 19.00, '2026-01-01', 'https://www.bundesfinanzministerium.de', true),
('US', 'CIT', 21.00, '2026-01-01', 'https://www.irs.gov', true),
('EU', 'VAT', 20.00, '2026-01-01', 'https://ec.europa.eu', true);
```

#### 7.3.4 迁移Makefile

```makefile
# Makefile
DATABASE_URL ?= postgres://taichu:taichu@localhost:5432/taichu_dev?sslmode=disable
MIGRATE := migrate -database "$(DATABASE_URL)" -path migrations

.PHONY: migrate-up migrate-down migrate-version migrate-force seed db-reset

migrate-up:
	$(MIGRATE) up

migrate-down:
	$(MIGRATE) down 1

migrate-version:
	$(MIGRATE) version

migrate-force:
	$(MIGRATE) force $(VERSION)

# 创建新迁移
migrate-create:
	migrate create -ext sql -dir migrations -seq $(NAME)

# 种子数据
seed:
	psql $(DATABASE_URL) -f migrations/seed/tax_rates.sql
	psql $(DATABASE_URL) -f migrations/seed/countries.sql

# 重置数据库（开发环境）
db-reset:
	$(MIGRATE) drop -f
	$(MIGRATE) up
	make seed

# 验证迁移
migrate-validate:
	$(MIGRATE) validate
```

#### 7.3.5 回滚策略

| 场景         | 策略         | 命令                                       |
| ------------ | ------------ | ------------------------------------------ |
| 开发环境错误 | 直接回滚     | `make migrate-down`                        |
| 生产环境错误 | 先备份再回滚 | `pg_dump → migrate-down → 验证`            |
| 破坏性变更   | 蓝绿部署     | 新schema并行运行 → 流量切换 → 旧schema删除 |
| 数据修复     | 补偿迁移     | 新建迁移脚本修复数据，不回滚               |
| 灾难恢复     | 时间点恢复   | WAL归档恢复到故障前一刻                    |

### 7.4 OpenAPI 3.1契约定义

#### 7.4.1 契约文件结构

```
/taichu-api/api/
├── openapi.yaml              # 根文件（仅包含info/servers/tags/security）
├── paths/
│   ├── users.yaml            # 用户相关路径
│   ├── companies.yaml        # 公司注册路径
│   ├── payments.yaml         # 支付路径
│   ├── ai.yaml               # AI服务路径
│   └── admin.yaml            # 管理员后台路径
├── schemas/
│   ├── user.yaml             # 用户模型
│   ├── company.yaml          # 公司模型
│   ├── payment.yaml          # 支付模型
│   ├── ai.yaml               # AI请求/响应模型
│   └── common.yaml           # 通用模型（分页/错误/元数据）
├── components/
│   ├── securitySchemes.yaml  # JWT/API Key定义
│   ├── parameters.yaml       # 通用参数（分页/排序/筛选）
│   └── responses.yaml        # 通用响应（401/403/500）
└── webhooks.yaml             # Webhook事件定义
```

#### 7.4.2 根文件示例

```yaml
# openapi.yaml
openapi: 3.1.0
info:
  title: 太初国链API
  description: 萨摩亚SPV × 海购星Dapp × 全球支付 × 超级AI大脑
  version: 1.0.0
  contact:
    name: 太初国链技术支持
    email: api@taichu.com
  license:
    name: Proprietary
    identifier: Proprietary

servers:
  - url: https://api.taichu.com/v1
    description: 生产环境
  - url: https://api-staging.taichu.com/v1
    description: 测试环境
  - url: http://localhost:8080/v1
    description: 本地开发

tags:
  - name: 认证
    description: 登录/注册/Token刷新
  - name: 用户
    description: 用户管理/KYC
  - name: 公司注册
    description: 萨摩亚公司注册全流程
  - name: 银行开户
    description: 香港银行开户协同
  - name: 支付
    description: 全球支付通道
  - name: AI大脑
    description: 税务计算/法务咨询/合同生成
  - name: 管理后台
    description: 管理员专用接口

security:
  - BearerAuth: []

paths:
  /auth/register:
    $ref: './paths/users.yaml#/paths/~1auth~1register'
  /auth/login:
    $ref: './paths/users.yaml#/paths/~1auth~1login'
  /users:
    $ref: './paths/users.yaml#/paths/~1users'
  /users/{id}:
    $ref: './paths/users.yaml#/paths/~1users~1{id}'
  /companies:
    $ref: './paths/companies.yaml#/paths/~1companies'
  /companies/{id}/submit:
    $ref: './paths/companies.yaml#/paths/~1companies~1{id}~1submit'
  /payments:
    $ref: './paths/payments.yaml#/paths/~1payments'
  /ai/tax-calculate:
    $ref: './paths/ai.yaml#/paths/~1ai~1tax-calculate'
  /ai/legal-contract:
    $ref: './paths/ai.yaml#/paths/~1ai~1legal-contract'
  /admin/users:
    $ref: './paths/admin.yaml#/paths/~1admin~1users'
  /admin/companies:
    $ref: './paths/admin.yaml#/paths/~1admin~1companies'
  /admin/transactions:
    $ref: './paths/admin.yaml#/paths/~1admin~1transactions'

components:
  securitySchemes:
    BearerAuth:
      type: http
      scheme: bearer
      bearerFormat: JWT
      description: Access Token，15分钟有效期
    ApiKeyAuth:
      type: apiKey
      in: header
      name: X-API-Key
      description: 第三方接入API Key

webhooks:
  companyRegistered:
    $ref: './webhooks.yaml#/webhooks/companyRegistered'
  paymentSuccess:
    $ref: './webhooks.yaml#/webhooks/paymentSuccess'
```

#### 7.4.3 路径定义示例

```yaml
# paths/companies.yaml
paths:
  /companies:
    get:
      summary: 查询公司列表
      tags: [公司注册]
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - $ref: '../components/parameters.yaml#/components/parameters/PageParam'
        - $ref: '../components/parameters.yaml#/components/parameters/PageSizeParam'
        - name: status
          in: query
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [draft, submitted, reviewing, registered, active, suspended]
        - name: sort
          in: query
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [created_at, -created_at, company_name_en]
      responses:
        '200':
          description: 成功
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                allOf:
                  - $ref: '../schemas/common.yaml#/schemas/SuccessResponse'
                  - properties:
                      data:
                        type: array
                        items:
                          $ref: '../schemas/company.yaml#/schemas/SamoaCompany'
        '401':
          $ref: '../components/responses.yaml#/components/responses/Unauthorized'
        '500':
          $ref: '../components/responses.yaml#/components/responses/InternalError'

    post:
      summary: 创建萨摩亚公司注册订单
      tags: [公司注册]
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '../schemas/company.yaml#/schemas/CreateCompanyRequest'
      responses:
        '201':
          description: 创建成功
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                allOf:
                  - $ref: '../schemas/common.yaml#/schemas/SuccessResponse'
                  - properties:
                      data:
                        $ref: '../schemas/company.yaml#/schemas/SamoaCompany'

  /companies/{id}/submit:
    post:
      summary: 提交注册资料至萨摩亚代理人
      tags: [公司注册]
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - name: id
          in: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
            format: uuid
      responses:
        '200':
          description: 提交成功
        '400':
          description: 资料不完整
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '../schemas/common.yaml#/schemas/ErrorResponse'
```

#### 7.4.4 Schema定义示例

```yaml
# schemas/company.yaml
schemas:
  SamoaCompany:
    type: object
    required: [id, user_id, company_name_en, status, created_at]
    properties:
      id:
        type: string
        format: uuid
      user_id:
        type: string
        format: uuid
      company_name_en:
        type: string
        maxLength: 255
      company_name_cn:
        type: string
        maxLength: 255
      company_number:
        type: string
        description: 萨摩亚注册处分配的公司编号
      registration_date:
        type: string
        format: date
      authorized_capital:
        type: number
        minimum: 10000
        maximum: 1000000
      business_type:
        type: string
        enum: [investment, trading, manufacturing, services, holding]
      status:
        type: string
        enum: [draft, submitted, reviewing, registered, active, suspended, dissolved]
      agent_id:
        type: string
        format: uuid
      annual_review_date:
        type: string
        format: date
      annual_review_status:
        type: string
        enum: [pending, completed, overdue]
      created_at:
        type: string
        format: date-time
      updated_at:
        type: string
        format: date-time

  CreateCompanyRequest:
    type: object
    required: [company_name_en, business_type, authorized_capital]
    properties:
      company_name_en:
        type: string
        maxLength: 255
      company_name_cn:
        type: string
        maxLength: 255
      business_type:
        type: string
        enum: [investment, trading, manufacturing, services, holding]
      business_description:
        type: string
        maxLength: 1000
      authorized_capital:
        type: number
        minimum: 10000
        maximum: 1000000
        default: 10000
      total_shares:
        type: integer
        default: 10000
      shareholders:
        type: array
        items:
          $ref: '#/schemas/ShareholderInfo'
      directors:
        type: array
        items:
          $ref: '#/schemas/DirectorInfo'

  ShareholderInfo:
    type: object
    required: [name, shares_held, is_corporate]
    properties:
      name:
        type: string
      shares_held:
        type: integer
      is_corporate:
        type: boolean
      corporation_details:
        type: object
        properties:
          place_of_incorporation:
            type: string
          company_number:
            type: string
```

#### 7.4.5 代码生成流水线

```yaml
# .github/workflows/openapi-codegen.yml
name: OpenAPI Code Generation

on:
  push:
    paths:
      - 'api/**'
  workflow_dispatch:

jobs:
  generate:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Validate OpenAPI
        run: |
          npx @redocly/cli lint api/openapi.yaml

      - name: Generate TypeScript Client
        run: |
          npx @openapitools/openapi-generator-cli generate             -i api/openapi.yaml             -g typescript-axios             -o packages/api-client/src             --additional-properties=supportsES6=true,npmName=@taichu/api-client

      - name: Generate Go Server Stub
        run: |
          npx @openapitools/openapi-generator-cli generate             -i api/openapi.yaml             -g go-gin-server             -o services/api/generated             --additional-properties=packageName=generated

      - name: Generate Documentation
        run: |
          npx @redocly/cli build-docs api/openapi.yaml -o docs/api.html

      - name: Commit Changes
        run: |
          git config user.name "github-actions"
          git config user.email "github-actions@github.com"
          git add packages/api-client/src services/api/generated docs/api.html
          git diff --cached --quiet || git commit -m "chore(api): 自动更新OpenAPI生成代码"
          git push
```

### 7.5 GitHub Actions地狱式审计流水线部署

#### 7.5.1 完整流水线配置

```yaml
# .github/workflows/hell-audit-v6.yml
name: Hell Audit Pipeline V6

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, develop, release/*]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main, release/*]
    types: [opened, synchronize, reopened, ready_for_review]
  schedule:
    - cron: '0 2 * * 1' # 每周一凌晨2点全量审计
    - cron: '0 */6 * * *' # 每6小时安全扫描

env:
  NODE_VERSION: '20.12.0'
  GO_VERSION: '1.22.0'
  PYTHON_VERSION: '3.11.0'
  PNPM_VERSION: '9.0.0'

concurrency:
  group: ${{ github.workflow }}-${{ github.ref }}
  cancel-in-progress: true

jobs:
  # ==========================================
  # Stage 1: 环境准备与依赖安装
  # ==========================================
  setup:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    outputs:
      changed-apps: ${{ steps.changes.outputs.apps }}
      changed-packages: ${{ steps.changes.outputs.packages }}
      changed-services: ${{ steps.changes.outputs.services }}
      changed-contracts: ${{ steps.changes.outputs.contracts }}
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
        with:
          fetch-depth: 0

      - name: Detect Changes
        id: changes
        uses: dorny/paths-filter@v3
        with:
          filters: |
            apps:
              - 'apps/**'
            packages:
              - 'packages/**'
            services:
              - 'services/**'
            contracts:
              - 'contracts/**'
            api:
              - 'api/**'
            migrations:
              - 'migrations/**'

      - name: Setup pnpm
        uses: pnpm/action-setup@v3
        with:
          version: ${{ env.PNPM_VERSION }}

      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: ${{ env.NODE_VERSION }}
          cache: 'pnpm'

      - name: Install Dependencies
        run: pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

      - name: Cache Dependencies
        uses: actions/cache@v4
        with:
          path: |
            node_modules
            ~/.local/share/pnpm/store
          key: ${{ runner.os }}-pnpm-${{ hashFiles('pnpm-lock.yaml') }}

  # ==========================================
  # Stage 2: 代码质量审计（L1自动化）
  # ==========================================
  lint-frontend:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: setup
    if: ${{ needs.setup.outputs.changed-apps == 'true' || needs.setup.outputs.changed-packages == 'true' }}
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: pnpm/action-setup@v3
        with:
          version: ${{ env.PNPM_VERSION }}
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: ${{ env.NODE_VERSION }}
          cache: 'pnpm'
      - run: pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

      - name: ESLint (Strict)
        run: pnpm run lint:strict

      - name: Prettier Check
        run: pnpm run format:check

      - name: TypeScript Check
        run: pnpm run type-check

      - name: Import Order Check
        run: pnpm run lint:imports

      - name: Complexity Report
        run: pnpm run lint:complexity

      - name: Upload Lint Report
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        if: always()
        with:
          name: lint-frontend-report
          path: reports/lint-frontend.json

  lint-backend:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: setup
    if: ${{ needs.setup.outputs.changed-services == 'true' }}
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-go@v5
        with:
          go-version: ${{ env.GO_VERSION }}

      - name: Go Vet
        run: |
          cd services/api
          go vet ./...

      - name: Go Fmt Check
        run: |
          cd services/api
          if [ -n "$(gofmt -l .)" ]; then
            echo "ERROR: 以下文件未格式化:"
            gofmt -l .
            exit 1
          fi

      - name: Go Cyclo Check
        run: |
          cd services/api
          go install github.com/fzipp/gocyclo/cmd/gocyclo@latest
          gocyclo -over 10 .

      - name: Go Test Race
        run: |
          cd services/api
          go test -race ./...

      - name: Go Coverage
        run: |
          cd services/api
          go test -coverprofile=coverage.out ./...
          go tool cover -func=coverage.out | tail -n 1

      - name: Upload Coverage
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        if: always()
        with:
          name: go-coverage-report
          path: services/api/coverage.out

  lint-ai:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: setup
    if: ${{ needs.setup.outputs.changed-services == 'true' }}
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: ${{ env.PYTHON_VERSION }}

      - name: Install Dependencies
        run: |
          cd services/ai
          pip install -r requirements-dev.txt

      - name: Ruff Lint
        run: |
          cd services/ai
          ruff check .

      - name: Ruff Format Check
        run: |
          cd services/ai
          ruff format --check .

      - name: MyPy Type Check
        run: |
          cd services/ai
          mypy app/

      - name: Pytest
        run: |
          cd services/ai
          pytest --cov=app --cov-report=xml

      - name: Upload Coverage
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        if: always()
        with:
          name: python-coverage-report
          path: services/ai/coverage.xml

  # ==========================================
  # Stage 3: 安全审计（L1自动化）
  # ==========================================
  security-sast:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: setup
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
        with:
          fetch-depth: 0

      - name: Semgrep SAST
        uses: returntocorp/semgrep-action@v1
        with:
          config: >-
            p/security-audit
            p/owasp-top-ten
            p/cwe-top-25
            p/ci
            p/command-injection
            p/sql-injection
            p/xss
            p/secrets

      - name: TruffleHog Secret Scan
        uses: trufflesecurity/trufflehog@main
        with:
          path: ./
          base: ${{ github.event.repository.default_branch }}
          head: HEAD
          extra_args: --debug --only-verified

      - name: GitLeaks Scan
        uses: gitleaks/gitleaks-action@v2
        env:
          GITHUB_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}

      - name: Upload Security Report
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        if: always()
        with:
          name: security-sast-report
          path: reports/security-sast.json

  security-sca:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: setup
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Snyk Node.js Scan
        uses: snyk/actions/node@master
        env:
          SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
        with:
          args: --severity-threshold=high --all-projects

      - name: Snyk Go Scan
        uses: snyk/actions/golang@master
        env:
          SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
        with:
          args: --severity-threshold=high

      - name: Snyk Python Scan
        uses: snyk/actions/python@master
        env:
          SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
        with:
          args: --severity-threshold=high --file=services/ai/requirements.txt

      - name: Trivy FS Scan
        uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
        with:
          scan-type: 'fs'
          scan-ref: '.'
          severity: 'CRITICAL,HIGH'
          format: 'sarif'
          output: 'trivy-results.sarif'

      - name: Upload Trivy Report
        uses: github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v3
        if: always()
        with:
          sarif_file: 'trivy-results.sarif'

  contract-security:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: setup
    if: ${{ needs.setup.outputs.changed-contracts == 'true' }}
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Slither Analysis
        uses: crytic/slither-action@v0.3.0
        with:
          target: 'contracts/solidity/'
          fail-on: 'high'
          slither-args: '--filter-paths "node_modules|openzeppelin"'

      - name: Mythril Analysis
        run: |
          pip install mythril
          myth analyze contracts/solidity/DVSToken.sol             --execution-timeout 600             --max-depth 50

      - name: Echidna Fuzzing
        run: |
          docker run -v $(pwd)/contracts:/src trailofbits/echidna             echidna /src/solidity/DVSToken.sol --contract DVSToken

  # ==========================================
  # Stage 4: 数据库审计（L1自动化）
  # ==========================================
  db-audit:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: setup
    if: ${{ needs.setup.outputs.changed-migrations == 'true' }}
    services:
      postgres:
        image: postgres:16-alpine
        env:
          POSTGRES_USER: taichu
          POSTGRES_PASSWORD: taichu
          POSTGRES_DB: taichu_test
        options: >-
          --health-cmd pg_isready
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
        ports:
          - 5432:5432
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Setup Go
        uses: actions/setup-go@v5
        with:
          go-version: ${{ env.GO_VERSION }}

      - name: Install golang-migrate
        run: |
          go install -tags postgres github.com/golang-migrate/migrate/v4/cmd/migrate@latest

      - name: Run Migrations
        env:
          DATABASE_URL: postgres://taichu:taichu@localhost:5432/taichu_test?sslmode=disable
        run: |
          migrate -database "$DATABASE_URL" -path migrations up

      - name: Schema Validation
        env:
          DATABASE_URL: postgres://taichu:taichu@localhost:5432/taichu_test?sslmode=disable
        run: |
          ./scripts/validate-schema.sh

      - name: Index Audit
        env:
          DATABASE_URL: postgres://taichu:taichu@localhost:5432/taichu_test?sslmode=disable
        run: |
          ./scripts/audit-indexes.sh

      - name: Migration Reversibility Test
        env:
          DATABASE_URL: postgres://taichu:taichu@localhost:5432/taichu_test?sslmode=disable
        run: |
          migrate -database "$DATABASE_URL" -path migrations down 1
          migrate -database "$DATABASE_URL" -path migrations up 1

      - name: Seed Data Test
        env:
          DATABASE_URL: postgres://taichu:taichu@localhost:5432/taichu_test?sslmode=disable
        run: |
          psql "$DATABASE_URL" -f migrations/seed/tax_rates.sql
          psql "$DATABASE_URL" -c "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ai.tax_rates;"

  # ==========================================
  # Stage 5: UI审计（L1自动化）
  # ==========================================
  ui-audit:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: setup
    if: ${{ needs.setup.outputs.changed-apps == 'true' || needs.setup.outputs.changed-packages == 'true' }}
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: pnpm/action-setup@v3
        with:
          version: ${{ env.PNPM_VERSION }}
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: ${{ env.NODE_VERSION }}
          cache: 'pnpm'
      - run: pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

      - name: Build Storybook
        run: pnpm run build-storybook

      - name: Serve Storybook
        run: |
          npx serve storybook-static -l 6006 &
          npx wait-on http://localhost:6006

      - name: axe-core Accessibility Scan
        run: |
          npx axe-core/cli http://localhost:6006             --tags wcag2a,wcag2aa,wcag21aa             --reporter v2             --output reports/a11y-report.json

      - name: Lighthouse CI
        run: |
          npm install -g @lhci/cli
          lhci autorun --config lighthouserc.js

      - name: Visual Regression (Chromatic)
        uses: chromaui/action@v11
        with:
          projectToken: ${{ secrets.CHROMATIC_PROJECT_TOKEN }}
          storybookBuildDir: storybook-static
          exitZeroOnChanges: true

      - name: Upload UI Reports
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        if: always()
        with:
          name: ui-audit-reports
          path: |
            reports/a11y-report.json
            .lighthouseci/

  # ==========================================
  # Stage 6: OpenAPI契约审计
  # ==========================================
  openapi-audit:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: setup
    if: ${{ needs.setup.outputs.changed-api == 'true' }}
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Validate OpenAPI
        run: |
          npx @redocly/cli lint api/openapi.yaml

      - name: Check Breaking Changes
        run: |
          npx @redocly/cli lint api/openapi.yaml             --extends recommended-strict

      - name: Generate and Verify Client
        run: |
          npx @openapitools/openapi-generator-cli generate             -i api/openapi.yaml             -g typescript-axios             -o /tmp/api-client-test
          cd /tmp/api-client-test
          npm install
          npm run build

  # ==========================================
  # Stage 7: 人工审查门禁（L2）
  # ==========================================
  peer-review-gate:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: [lint-frontend, lint-backend, security-sast, db-audit, ui-audit]
    if: github.event_name == 'pull_request'
    steps:
      - name: Check Minimum Reviewers
        run: |
          REVIEWERS=$(curl -s -H "Authorization: token ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}"             "https://api.github.com/repos/${{ github.repository }}/pulls/${{ github.event.pull_request.number }}/requested_reviewers"             | jq '.users | length')
          if [ "$REVIEWERS" -lt 2 ]; then
            echo "ERROR: 需要至少2名审查者，当前: $REVIEWERS"
            exit 1
          fi
          echo "审查者数量: $REVIEWERS ✅"

      - name: Check Review Approvals
        run: |
          APPROVALS=$(curl -s -H "Authorization: token ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}"             "https://api.github.com/repos/${{ github.repository }}/pulls/${{ github.event.pull_request.number }}/reviews"             | jq '[.[] | select(.state == "APPROVED")] | length')
          if [ "$APPROVALS" -lt 2 ]; then
            echo "ERROR: 需要至少2个Approve，当前: $APPROVALS"
            exit 1
          fi
          echo "Approve数量: $APPROVALS ✅"

      - name: Check Unresolved Conversations
        run: |
          UNRESOLVED=$(curl -s -H "Authorization: token ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}"             "https://api.github.com/repos/${{ github.repository }}/pulls/${{ github.event.pull_request.number }}/comments"             | jq '[.[] | select(.state != "resolved")] | length')
          if [ "$UNRESOLVED" -gt 0 ]; then
            echo "ERROR: 有 $UNRESOLVED 条未解决对话"
            exit 1
          fi
          echo "无未解决对话 ✅"

  # ==========================================
  # Stage 8: 审计报告汇总
  # ==========================================
  audit-report:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs:
      [
        lint-frontend,
        lint-backend,
        lint-ai,
        security-sast,
        security-sca,
        contract-security,
        db-audit,
        ui-audit,
        openapi-audit,
      ]
    if: always()
    steps:
      - name: Generate Comprehensive Audit Report
        run: |
          cat > audit-report-v6.md << 'EOF'
          # 太初国链 · 地狱式审计报告 V6

          | 检查项 | 状态 | 详情 |
          |--------|------|------|
          | 前端Lint | ${{ needs.lint-frontend.result }} | ESLint/Prettier/TypeScript |
          | 后端Lint | ${{ needs.lint-backend.result }} | Go Vet/Fmt/Cyclo/Race |
          | AI服务Lint | ${{ needs.lint-ai.result }} | Ruff/MyPy/Pytest |
          | SAST扫描 | ${{ needs.security-sast.result }} | Semgrep/TruffleHog/GitLeaks |
          | SCA扫描 | ${{ needs.security-sca.result }} | Snyk/Trivy |
          | 合约安全 | ${{ needs.contract-security.result }} | Slither/Mythril/Echidna |
          | 数据库审计 | ${{ needs.db-audit.result }} | Schema/Index/迁移 |
          | UI审计 | ${{ needs.ui-audit.result }} | axe-core/Lighthouse/Chromatic |
          | OpenAPI审计 | ${{ needs.openapi-audit.result }} | Redocly/生成验证 |

          **总体状态**: ${{ (contains(needs.*.result, 'failure') && '❌ 未通过') || '✅ 通过' }}
          **生成时间**: $(date -u +"%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ")
          **提交**: ${{ github.sha }}
          **分支**: ${{ github.ref }}
          **触发**: ${{ github.event_name }}
          EOF

      - name: Upload Final Report
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: hell-audit-report-v6
          path: audit-report-v6.md

      - name: Comment on PR
        if: github.event_name == 'pull_request'
        uses: actions/github-script@v7
        with:
          script: |
            const fs = require('fs');
            const report = fs.readFileSync('audit-report-v6.md', 'utf8');
            github.rest.issues.createComment({
              issue_number: context.issue.number,
              owner: context.repo.owner,
              repo: context.repo.repo,
              body: report
            });
```

#### 7.5.2 审计门禁矩阵

| 阶段            | 触发条件      | 必须通过                                  | 未通过后果               |
| --------------- | ------------- | ----------------------------------------- | ------------------------ |
| **pre-commit**  | `git commit`  | ESLint + Prettier + 单元测试              | Husky阻止提交            |
| **PR创建**      | 推送至PR分支  | L1全部通过（Lint/Security/DB/UI/OpenAPI） | CI状态失败，禁止合并     |
| **PR合并**      | 点击Merge     | 2名审查者Approve + 0未解决对话            | GitHub分支保护阻止合并   |
| **Staging部署** | 合并至develop | 安全扫描无Critical/High                   | 部署流水线中断           |
| **生产部署**    | 合并至main    | 全量审计通过 + CTO手动审批                | 禁止生产部署             |
| **季度审计**    | 定时触发      | L3外部安全审计通过                        | 暂停新功能开发，专注修复 |
| **年度审计**    | 定时触发      | L4合规审计通过                            | 业务牌照风险             |

---

## 八、管理员后台详细设计

### 8.1 后台数据库表设计

```sql
-- 管理员账户表（独立于用户表，更高权限）
CREATE TABLE admin.accounts (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES user.users(id),
    username VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    role VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (role IN ('super_admin', 'admin', 'agent', 'bank_partner', 'support')),
    permissions JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}', -- 细粒度权限矩阵
    department VARCHAR(50),
    last_active_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- 操作日志表（管理员行为全记录）
CREATE TABLE admin.operation_logs (
    id BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    admin_id UUID REFERENCES admin.accounts(id),
    action VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- 如: approve_kyc, reject_company, refund_payment
    target_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- 如: user, company, payment
    target_id UUID NOT NULL,
    old_values JSONB,
    new_values JSONB,
    ip_address INET,
    user_agent TEXT,
    reason TEXT, -- 操作理由
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- 系统配置表（动态配置，无需重启）
CREATE TABLE admin.system_configs (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    config_key VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    config_value TEXT NOT NULL,
    config_type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (config_type IN ('string', 'number', 'boolean', 'json')),
    description TEXT,
    is_sensitive BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
    updated_by UUID REFERENCES admin.accounts(id),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- 银行渠道配置表
CREATE TABLE admin.bank_channels (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    bank_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    bank_code VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    country VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    account_types JSONB NOT NULL, -- ['corporate', 'offshore', 'multi-currency']
    min_deposit DECIMAL(15, 2),
    monthly_fee DECIMAL(10, 2),
    supported_currencies JSONB,
    requires_visit BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
    supported_visit_types JSONB, -- ['hk_branch', 'mainland_witness', 'video_remote']
    processing_days_min INT,
    processing_days_max INT,
    success_rate DECIMAL(5, 2), -- 历史成功率
    status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'active' CHECK (status IN ('active', 'paused', 'deprecated')),
    api_config JSONB, -- 对接API配置（加密存储）
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- 支付渠道配置表
CREATE TABLE admin.payment_channels (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    channel_code VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    channel_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    channel_type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (channel_type IN ('credit_card', 'local_wallet', 'crypto', 'bank_wire', 'aggregator')),
    supported_countries JSONB,
    supported_currencies JSONB,
    fee_rate DECIMAL(5, 4) NOT NULL, -- 手续费率
    settlement_period VARCHAR(20), -- T+1, T+3等
    min_amount DECIMAL(15, 2),
    max_amount DECIMAL(15, 2),
    api_endpoint VARCHAR(500),
    webhook_url VARCHAR(500),
    api_key_encrypted TEXT, -- 加密存储
    api_secret_encrypted TEXT, -- 加密存储
    status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'active',
    health_check_url VARCHAR(500),
    last_health_check_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    last_health_status VARCHAR(20),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- AI知识库管理表
CREATE TABLE admin.ai_knowledge_entries (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    category VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL CHECK (category IN ('tax', 'legal', 'compliance', 'contract', 'sanctions')),
    subcategory VARCHAR(50),
    country VARCHAR(50),
    title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    content TEXT NOT NULL,
    content_vector_id VARCHAR(100), -- Milvus向量ID
    source_url VARCHAR(500),
    source_document VARCHAR(500),
    effective_date DATE,
    expiry_date DATE,
    verified_by UUID REFERENCES admin.accounts(id),
    verified_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending' CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'verified', 'outdated', 'rejected')),
    version INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
    previous_version_id UUID REFERENCES admin.ai_knowledge_entries(id),
    created_by UUID REFERENCES admin.accounts(id),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- 制裁名单表（实时更新）
CREATE TABLE admin.sanctions_lists (
    id BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    list_source VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (list_source IN ('OFAC', 'UN', 'EU', 'HMT', 'CN')),
    entity_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    entity_type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (entity_type IN ('individual', 'company', 'vessel', 'aircraft')),
    aliases JSONB,
    addresses JSONB,
    identification_numbers JSONB,
    programs JSONB, -- 制裁项目
    effective_date DATE,
    removed_date DATE,
    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
    raw_data JSONB, -- 原始数据备份
    last_synced_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    UNIQUE(list_source, entity_name)
);
```

### 8.2 后台API设计

```yaml
# api/paths/admin.yaml
paths:
  /admin/dashboard:
    get:
      summary: 仪表盘数据
      tags: [管理后台-仪表盘]
      security: [BearerAuth: []]
      responses:
        '200':
          description: 仪表盘KPI数据
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: object
                properties:
                  today:
                    type: object
                    properties:
                      new_users: { type: integer }
                      new_companies: { type: integer }
                      new_payments: { type: integer }
                      revenue: { type: number }
                  trends:
                    type: object
                    properties:
                      users_7d: { type: array, items: { type: object } }
                      revenue_30d: { type: array, items: { type: object } }
                  alerts:
                    type: array
                    items:
                      type: object
                      properties:
                        level: { type: string, enum: [critical, warning, info] }
                        message: { type: string }
                        created_at: { type: string, format: date-time }

  /admin/users:
    get:
      summary: 用户列表（管理员视角）
      tags: [管理后台-用户管理]
      security: [BearerAuth: []]
      parameters:
        - name: kyc_status
          in: query
          schema: { type: string, enum: [pending, reviewing, approved, rejected] }
        - name: dlc_level
          in: query
          schema: { type: integer, minimum: 1, maximum: 9 }
        - name: registration_date_from
          in: query
          schema: { type: string, format: date }
        - name: registration_date_to
          in: query
          schema: { type: string, format: date }
      responses:
        '200':
          description: 用户列表（含KYC状态、DLC等级、公司数量）

  /admin/users/{id}/kyc:
    post:
      summary: KYC审核操作
      tags: [管理后台-用户管理]
      security: [BearerAuth: []]
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              required: [action]
              properties:
                action: { type: string, enum: [approve, reject, request_info] }
                reason: { type: string }
                requested_documents: { type: array, items: { type: string } }
      responses:
        '200':
          description: 审核操作成功

  /admin/companies:
    get:
      summary: 公司注册订单列表
      tags: [管理后台-公司注册]
      security: [BearerAuth: []]
      parameters:
        - name: status
          in: query
          schema:
            { type: string, enum: [draft, submitted, reviewing, registered, active, suspended] }
        - name: agent_id
          in: query
          schema: { type: string, format: uuid }
        - name: annual_review_overdue
          in: query
          schema: { type: boolean }
      responses:
        '200':
          description: 公司订单列表

  /admin/companies/{id}/review:
    post:
      summary: 资料审核
      tags: [管理后台-公司注册]
      security: [BearerAuth: []]
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              required: [action]
              properties:
                action: { type: string, enum: [approve, reject, request_docs] }
                missing_documents: { type: array, items: { type: string } }
                notes: { type: string }
      responses:
        '200':
          description: 审核完成

  /admin/payments/channels:
    get:
      summary: 支付通道列表
      tags: [管理后台-全球支付]
      security: [BearerAuth: []]
      responses:
        '200':
          description: 通道配置列表
    post:
      summary: 新增支付通道
      tags: [管理后台-全球支付]
      security: [BearerAuth: []]
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '../schemas/admin.yaml#/schemas/PaymentChannelConfig'

  /admin/payments/channels/{id}/health:
    post:
      summary: 手动健康检查
      tags: [管理后台-全球支付]
      security: [BearerAuth: []]
      responses:
        '200':
          description: 健康检查结果

  /admin/ai/knowledge:
    get:
      summary: AI知识库条目列表
      tags: [管理后台-AI大脑]
      security: [BearerAuth: []]
      parameters:
        - name: category
          in: query
          schema: { type: string, enum: [tax, legal, compliance, contract, sanctions] }
        - name: status
          in: query
          schema: { type: string, enum: [pending, verified, outdated] }
        - name: verified_only
          in: query
          schema: { type: boolean }
      responses:
        '200':
          description: 知识库条目列表
    post:
      summary: 新增知识库条目
      tags: [管理后台-AI大脑]
      security: [BearerAuth: []]
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              required: [category, title, content]
              properties:
                category: { type: string }
                country: { type: string }
                title: { type: string }
                content: { type: string }
                source_url: { type: string }
                effective_date: { type: string, format: date }

  /admin/ai/knowledge/{id}/verify:
    post:
      summary: 核验知识库条目
      tags: [管理后台-AI大脑]
      security: [BearerAuth: []]
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              required: [status]
              properties:
                status: { type: string, enum: [verified, outdated, rejected] }
                notes: { type: string }
      responses:
        '200':
          description: 核验完成

  /admin/legal/sanctions:
    get:
      summary: 制裁名单查询
      tags: [管理后台-税务法务]
      security: [BearerAuth: []]
      parameters:
        - name: list_source
          in: query
          schema: { type: string, enum: [OFAC, UN, EU, HMT, CN] }
        - name: entity_name
          in: query
          schema: { type: string }
        - name: is_active
          in: query
          schema: { type: boolean }
      responses:
        '200':
          description: 制裁名单查询结果
    post:
      summary: 手动同步制裁名单
      tags: [管理后台-税务法务]
      security: [BearerAuth: []]
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              required: [list_source]
              properties:
                list_source: { type: string, enum: [OFAC, UN, EU, HMT, CN] }
      responses:
        '200':
          description: 同步任务已启动
```

### 8.3 后台组件库详细清单

| 组件类别     | 组件名称           | 功能说明                                          | 使用场景      |
| ------------ | ------------------ | ------------------------------------------------- | ------------- |
| **数据展示** | StatCard           | KPI卡片（标题+数值+趋势+图标）                    | 仪表盘        |
|              | ChartLine          | 折线图（多系列+时间轴+缩放）                      | 营收趋势      |
|              | ChartBar           | 柱状图（分组+堆叠+动画）                          | Agent调用量   |
|              | ChartPie           | 饼图（环形+图例+点击下钻）                        | 订单分布      |
|              | ChartRadar         | 雷达图（多维度+对比）                             | 合规评分      |
|              | DataTable          | 高级表格（排序/筛选/分页/导出/批量操作）          | 所有列表页    |
|              | Timeline           | 时间线（图标+状态+描述+操作）                     | 注册/开户进度 |
|              | StatusBadge        | 状态标签（颜色+图标+文字）                        | 状态展示      |
| **表单**     | FormSection        | 分组表单区块（标题+折叠）                         | 复杂表单      |
|              | InputKYC           | 证件输入（类型切换+号码校验+OCR提示）             | KYC审核       |
|              | UploadCertified    | 核证副本上传（拖拽+预览+日期检查+水印）           | 资料审核      |
|              | SelectCountry      | 国家选择器（搜索+国旗+税率提示）                  | 税务计算      |
|              | AIChatEmbed        | 内嵌AI对话（侧边栏+历史+快捷指令）                | 知识库管理    |
|              | SearchFilter       | 高级筛选（多条件+保存模板+重置）                  | 列表页        |
| **反馈**     | AlertBanner        | 顶部告警横幅（级别+标题+操作+关闭）               | 全局告警      |
|              | Toast              | 全局通知（位置+动画+自动关闭）                    | 操作反馈      |
|              | ModalConfirm       | 确认弹窗（危险操作+二次确认+理由输入）            | 删除/拒绝     |
|              | ProgressStep       | 多步骤进度条（可点击+状态+描述）                  | 注册流程      |
|              | EmptyState         | 空状态（插图+标题+描述+操作）                     | 无数据        |
| **导航**     | SidebarNav         | 可折叠侧边栏（图标+文字+徽章+子菜单）             | 后台导航      |
|              | Breadcrumb         | 面包屑（首页+路径+当前+点击返回）                 | 页面定位      |
|              | TabGroup           | 标签页（滑动+徽章+关闭+记忆）                     | 详情页        |
|              | StickyCTA          | 固定底部行动栏（主按钮+次按钮+信息）              | 表单页        |
| **业务专用** | KYCReviewPanel     | KYC审核面板（资料预览+通过/拒绝+备注）            | KYC审核页     |
|              | CompanyTimeline    | 公司注册时间线（节点+状态+文件+操作）             | 注册订单详情  |
|              | PaymentChannelCard | 支付通道卡片（图标+状态+费率+健康度+操作）        | 通道管理      |
|              | TaxRateEditor      | 税率编辑器（国家/税种/税率/生效日期/来源）        | 税率数据库    |
|              | SanctionsTable     | 制裁名单表格（来源/实体/类型/别名/状态/同步时间） | 制裁名单管理  |
|              | AIKnowledgeCard    | 知识库卡片（分类/标题/摘要/状态/核验按钮）        | 知识库管理    |
|              | DLCTierManager     | DLC等级管理器（等级/条件/特权/图标/权重）         | 会员等级      |
|              | DVSFPoolMonitor    | 分红池监控（池余额/分配比例/发放记录/图表）       | 分红池管理    |

### 8.4 后台页面详细规格

#### 页面：仪表盘（Dashboard）

```
布局：全宽，顶部KPI行 + 中部图表区 + 底部告警区

KPI行（4列）：
┌─────────────┐ ┌─────────────┐ ┌─────────────┐ ┌─────────────┐
│ 今日新用户    │ │ 今日新注册    │ │ 今日营收      │ │ AI对话量     │
│  128 ↑12%    │ │  23 ↑5%      │ │ $45,230 ↑8% │ │ 1,234 ↑23%  │
│ [趋势迷你图]  │ │ [趋势迷你图]  │ │ [趋势迷你图]  │ │ [趋势迷你图]  │
└─────────────┘ └─────────────┘ └─────────────┘ └─────────────┘

图表区（2×2网格）：
┌─────────────────────┐ ┌─────────────────────┐
│ 营收趋势（30天）     │ │ 用户增长漏斗        │
│ [ECharts折线图]      │ │ [ECharts漏斗图]     │
│ 同比/环比切换        │ │ 转化率标注          │
└─────────────────────┘ └─────────────────────┘
┌─────────────────────┐ ┌─────────────────────┐
│ 注册订单状态分布     │ │ AI Agent调用TOP5   │
│ [ECharts饼图]        │ │ [ECharts条形图]     │
│ 点击下钻详情        │ │ 实时跳动            │
└─────────────────────┘ └─────────────────────┘

告警区（底部全宽）：
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ 实时告警                                                    │
│ 🔴 [CRITICAL] 3单注册资料缺护照扫描件（超24小时未处理）      │
│ 🟡 [WARNING] 1笔加密支付异常（单笔$50k+，触发风控）            │
│ 🔵 [INFO] 萨摩亚税率数据库已更新（2026-06-05 14:30）        │
│ [查看全部告警]                                              │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

#### 页面：支付通道管理（Payment Channels）

```

操作栏：
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ [+ 新增通道]  [批量启用]  [批量禁用]  [导出配置]              │

卡片网格（每行3列）：
┌────────────────────────────────────────┐

│ ━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━  │
│ 健康度：98%  最后检查：2分钟前           │
│ 本月流水：$1.2M  成功率：99.2%         │
│ ━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━  │
│ [配置]  [测试]  [查看日志]  [禁用]      │
└────────────────────────────────────────┘

┌────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ 🔗 USDT-TRC20                          │
│ 类型：加密数字  状态：✅ 正常            │
│ ━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━  │
│ 链：Tron  合约：TR7NHq...               │
│ 费率：0.5%（网络费另计）                 │
│ 结算：实时                               │
│ 限额：$10 - $500,000/笔                 │
│ ━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━  │
│ 热钱包余额：$234,500                    │
│ 冷钱包余额：$1,200,000                  │
│ 本月流水：$3.4M  交易数：1,234          │
│ ━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━  │
│ [配置]  [轮换地址]  [查看链上]  [禁用]   │
└────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

#### 页面：AI知识库管理（AI Knowledge Base）

```
布局：左侧分类树 + 右侧内容区

左侧分类树：
┌────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ 📚 AI知识库                             │
│ ━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━  │
│ 📁 税务知识                              │
│   ├─ 🇨🇳 中国（15条）                    │
│   ├─ 🇭🇰 香港（8条）                    │
│   ├─ 🇼🇸 萨摩亚（12条）                  │

│   ├─ 🇪🇺 欧盟GDPR（10条）                │
│   ├─ 🇺🇸 美国CCPA（8条）                 │
│   └─ 🇨🇳 中国PIPL（5条）                 │

右侧内容区（选中"中国税务"）：
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ 🇨🇳 中国税务知识  [+ 新增条目]  [批量导入]  [导出]           │
│ ━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━  │
│ 筛选：状态 [全部 ▼] 核验 [全部 ▼] 搜索 [________]            │
│                                                            │
│ ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐│
│ │ 企业所得税（CIT）                                        ││
│ │ 税率：25%  生效：2026-01-01  状态：✅ 已核验             ││
│ │ 来源：国税总局  核验人：Admin_01  核验时间：2026-05-01  ││
│ │ 摘要：一般企业25%，高新技术企业15%，海南自贸港鼓励类15%   ││
│ │ [查看详情]  [编辑]  [版本历史]  [向量检索测试]            ││
│ └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘│
│ ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐│
│ │ 增值税（VAT）                                            ││
│ │ 税率：13%/9%/6%  生效：2026-01-01  状态：⏳ 待核验       ││
│ │ 来源：国税总局  提交人：AI_Crawler  提交时间：2026-06-05││
│ │ 摘要：出口货物退税率13%/9%，跨境电商综试区免税政策...     ││
│ │ [查看详情]  [✅ 核验通过]  [❌ 驳回]  [编辑]             ││
│ └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘│
│                                                            │
│ 分页：<< < 1 2 3 ... 15 > >>  共 142 条                   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

# 8.5 新增后台独立页面线框图

> 本章为太初国链管理员后台（Admin Dashboard）新增独立页面提供完整的UI线框设计、组件规格与交互定义。所有线框基于 **React 18 + Ant Design Pro v5 + 深色模式（Dark Theme）** 绘制，色彩变量遵循 Ant Design 官方暗色令牌（`colorBgBase: #141414`、`colorBgContainer: #1f1f1f`、`colorBorder: #434343`）。

> **文档版本**: v1.0 | **适用产品版本**: 太初国链 Admin Dashboard v2.5+ | **技术栈**: React 18 + Ant Design Pro v5 + TypeScript + Recharts + WebSocket

---

## 8.5.1 公司注册订单管理页

### 页面概览

公司注册订单管理页是后台运营核心模块，承载全球公司注册订单的全生命周期管理。页面采用 **筛选栏 → 统计卡片区 → 批量操作栏 → 表格主体** 的四层纵向布局，支持多维度筛选、状态聚合与批量操作。面向运营团队、代理人主管和合规审核员三类角色，通过权限控制展示差异化操作。

### 完整线框图（1440×900 视口）


### 表格列定义（TypeScript）

```typescript
interface CompanyOrderColumn {
  orderNo: string;              // 订单号，格式 REG-{YY}{NNNNN}
  companyEn: string;            // 公司英文名
  companyCn: string;            // 公司中文名
  applicant: string;            // 申请人姓名
  applicantId: string;          // 申请人用户ID
  applicantAvatar?: string;     // 申请人头像
  status: 'pending' | 'reviewing' | 'registered' | 'supplement' | 'rejected' | 'expiring';
  submitTime: string;           // ISO 8601
  agentName: string;            // 代理人名称
  agentId: string;
  agentAvatar?: string;
  jurisdiction: string;         // 注册地: HK / SG / US / UK / WS
  companyType: string;
  reviewerNotes?: string;
  attachments: Attachment[];
  timeline: TimelineEvent[];
}

interface Attachment {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  type: string;
  size: number;
  status: 'uploaded' | 'missing' | 'pending_review';
  url: string;
  uploadedAt: string;
}

interface TimelineEvent {
  id: string;
  status: string;
  operator: string;
  timestamp: string;
  note?: string;
}

const columns: ProColumns<CompanyOrderColumn>[] = [
  {
    title: '订单号',
    dataIndex: 'orderNo',
    width: 130,
    fixed: 'left',
    sorter: true,
    render: (text) => <Tag color="blue" style={{ fontFamily: 'monospace' }}>{text}</Tag>,
  },
  {
    title: '公司名',
    dataIndex: 'companyEn',
    width: 260,
    ellipsis: true,
    render: (_, record) => (
      <div>
        <div style={{ fontWeight: 600, fontSize: 14 }}>{record.companyEn}</div>
        {record.companyCn && (
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: '#8C8C8C', marginTop: 2 }}>{record.companyCn}</div>
        )}
        <div style={{ marginTop: 4 }}>
          <Tag size="small">{getJurisdictionFlag(record.jurisdiction)} {record.jurisdiction}</Tag>
        </div>
      </div>
    ),
  },
  {
    title: '申请人',
    dataIndex: 'applicant',
    width: 120,
    render: (text, record) => (
      <Space><Avatar size="small" src={record.applicantAvatar} /><span>{text}</span></Space>
    ),
  },
  {
    title: '状态',
    dataIndex: 'status',
    width: 110,
    filters: true,
    onFilter: true,
    valueEnum: {
      pending: { text: '待审核', status: 'Warning' },
      reviewing: { text: '审核中', status: 'Processing' },
      registered: { text: '已注册', status: 'Success' },
      supplement: { text: '需补件', status: 'Error' },
      rejected: { text: '已驳回', status: 'Default' },
      expiring: { text: '年审到期', status: 'Warning' },
    },
  },
  {
    title: '提交时间',
    dataIndex: 'submitTime',
    width: 160,
    sorter: true,
    render: (text) => (
      <Tooltip title={dayjs(text).format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss')}>
        {dayjs(text).format('MM-DD HH:mm')}
      </Tooltip>
    ),
  },
  {
    title: '代理人',
    dataIndex: 'agentName',
    width: 120,
    filters: true,
    onFilter: true,
    render: (text, record) => (
      <Space><Avatar size="small" src={record.agentAvatar} /><span>{text}</span></Space>
    ),
  },
  {
    title: '操作',
    valueType: 'option',
    width: 220,
    fixed: 'right',
    render: (_, record) => (
      <Space size="small">
        <Button key="view" size="small" icon={<EyeOutlined />} onClick={() => showDetailDrawer(record)}>查看</Button>
        {record.status === 'pending' && (
          <Button key="audit" size="small" type="primary" icon={<EditOutlined />} onClick={() => openAuditModal(record)}>审核</Button>
        )}
        <Button key="remind" size="small" icon={<BellOutlined />} onClick={() => sendReminder(record)}>催办</Button>
        <Dropdown key="more" overlay={moreMenu(record)}>
          <Button size="small" icon={<MoreOutlined />} />
        </Dropdown>
      </Space>
    ),
  },
];
```

### 状态标签颜色映射（深色模式）

| 状态值       | 徽章类型     | 背景色    | 文字色    | 触发条件         | 对应操作      |
| ------------ | ------------ | --------- | --------- | ---------------- | ------------- |
| `pending`    | `Warning`    | `#2B1D11` | `#D46B08` | 用户提交资料后   | 审核/催办     |
| `reviewing`  | `Processing` | `#1D2B2B` | `#5BD4D0` | 代理人开始审核   | 查看/转交     |
| `registered` | `Success`    | `#1B2E1B` | `#5BD46E` | 政府完成注册     | 查看/年审设置 |
| `supplement` | `Error`      | `#2E1B1B` | `#D45050` | 审核发现资料缺失 | 催办/驳回     |
| `rejected`   | `Default`    | `#262626` | `#8C8C8C` | 严重不合规       | 归档/重新申请 |
| `expiring`   | `Warning`    | `#2B1D11` | `#D46B08` | 年审即将到期     | 年审提醒      |

### 权限矩阵

| 功能           | 超级管理员 | 运营主管 | 审核员 | 代理人       | 只读账号 |
| -------------- | ---------- | -------- | ------ | ------------ | -------- |
| 查看订单列表   | ✅         | ✅       | ✅     | ✅(仅自己的) | ✅(脱敏) |
| 审核订单       | ✅         | ✅       | ✅     | ❌           | ❌       |
| 批量导出       | ✅         | ✅       | ❌     | ❌           | ❌       |
| 批量分配代理人 | ✅         | ✅       | ❌     | ❌           | ❌       |
| 发送催办       | ✅         | ✅       | ✅     | ✅(仅自己的) | ❌       |
| 驳回/删除      | ✅         | ✅       | ✅     | ❌           | ❌       |
| 查看统计卡片   | ✅         | ✅       | ✅     | ✅(仅自己的) | ✅(部分) |
| 高级筛选       | ✅         | ✅       | ✅     | ✅(部分)     | ✅(部分) |

### API 接口

```typescript
// 获取订单列表
GET /api/admin/company-orders
Params: {
  status?: 'pending' | 'reviewing' | 'registered' | 'supplement' | 'rejected' | 'expiring';
  submitDateStart?: string; submitDateEnd?: string;
  agentId?: string; companyName?: string; jurisdiction?: string;
  page?: number; pageSize?: number; sortField?: string; sortOrder?: 'ascend' | 'descend';
}
Response: { data: CompanyOrder[]; total: number;
  summary: { pending: number; reviewing: number; registered: number; expiring: number; };
}

// 批量操作
POST /api/admin/company-orders/batch
Body: { action: 'export' | 'assign_agent' | 'send_reminder'; ids: string[]; params: Record<string, any>; }

// 审核订单
POST /api/admin/company-orders/:id/audit
Body: { action: 'approve' | 'reject' | 'request_supplement'; notes: string; attachments?: string[]; }

// 发送催办
POST /api/admin/company-orders/:id/remind
Body: { channels: ('email' | 'sms' | 'app')[]; message?: string; }
```

---

## 8.5.2 银行开户申请管理页

### 页面概览

银行开户申请管理页处理企业银行账户开设的全流程，集成香港、新加坡、美国等多地区银行的开户申请。核心特性包括多银行筛选、开户模式区分（内地见证/赴港/远程视频）、详情抽屉审核、退款管理子模块。与公司注册订单形成上下游关系——通常公司注册完成后才发起银行开户。

### 完整线框图

```
+==========================================================================================+
| [Logo] 太初国链 Admin                        [🔍] [🔔12] [👤 Admin ▼]    Dark Theme      |
+==========================================================================================+
| [Sidebar]      |                                                                         |
|                |  Breadcrumb: 首页 / 订单管理 / 银行开户申请                               |

|                |  │ ┌───────────┐ ┌──────────────┐ ┌────────┐ ┌──────────────────────┐ │ |
|                |  │ │银行 ▼全部  │ │模式 ▼全部    │ │状态 ▼  │ │🔍 搜索公司名/申请号  │ │ |
|                |  │ └───────────┘ └──────────────┘ └────────┘ └──────────────────────┘ │ |
```

### 详情抽屉线框图（720px）

### 开户状态机定义

```typescript
type BankApplicationStatus =
  | 'submitted'
  | 'preliminary_review'
  | 'document_review'
  | 'appointment_scheduled'
  | 'appointment_done'
  | 'bank_review'
  | 'approved'
  | 'rejected'
  | 'refund_pending'
  | 'refunded'
  | 'cancelled';

const statusFlow: Record<BankApplicationStatus, BankApplicationStatus[]> = {
  submitted: ['preliminary_review', 'cancelled'],
  preliminary_review: ['document_review', 'rejected', 'cancelled'],
  document_review: ['appointment_scheduled', 'rejected'],
  appointment_scheduled: ['appointment_done', 'cancelled'],
  appointment_done: ['bank_review'],
  bank_review: ['approved', 'rejected'],
  approved: ['refund_pending'],
  rejected: ['refund_pending'],
  refund_pending: ['refunded'],
  refunded: [],
  cancelled: ['refund_pending'],
};

const statusColorMap: Record<BankApplicationStatus, { bg: string; text: string }> = {
  submitted: { bg: '#1D2B2B', text: '#5BD4D0' },
  preliminary_review: { bg: '#2B1D11', text: '#D46B08' },
  document_review: { bg: '#1D2B2B', text: '#5BD4D0' },
  appointment_scheduled: { bg: '#1D1D2B', text: '#5B7BD4' },
  appointment_done: { bg: '#1D1D2B', text: '#5B7BD4' },
  bank_review: { bg: '#1D2B2B', text: '#5BD4D0' },
  approved: { bg: '#1B2E1B', text: '#5BD46E' },
  rejected: { bg: '#2E1B1B', text: '#D45050' },
  refund_pending: { bg: '#2B1D11', text: '#D46B08' },
  refunded: { bg: '#262626', text: '#8C8C8C' },
  cancelled: { bg: '#262626', text: '#8C8C8C' },
};

interface BankApplication {
  applicationNo: string;
  companyName: string;
  companyEnName: string;
  bankCode: string;
  bankName: string;
  openMode: 'witness' | 'visit_hk' | 'remote';
  status: BankApplicationStatus;
  submitTime: string;
  appointment?: {
    scheduledAt: string;
    branchName: string;
    branchAddress: string;
    accountManager?: string;
    managerContact?: string;
    mode: string;
    status: 'confirmed' | 'pending' | 'cancelled';
  };
  questionnaire: { questionId: string; question: string; answer: string; category: string }[];
  refundRecords: RefundRecord[];
}

interface RefundRecord {
  refundNo: string;
  amount: number;
  currency: string;
  status:
    | 'pending_ops'
    | 'pending_finance'
    | 'pending_exec'
    | 'approved'
    | 'rejected'
    | 'processed';
  appliedBy: string;
  appliedAt: string;
  reason: string;
  approvalChain: {
    step: string;
    status: string;
    operator?: string;
    operatedAt?: string;
    comment?: string;
  }[];
  processedAt?: string;
  transactionRef?: string;
}
```

### 权限矩阵

| 功能           | 超级管理员 | 运营主管 | 审核员 | 代理人       | 只读账号 |
| -------------- | ---------- | -------- | ------ | ------------ | -------- |
| 查看申请列表   | ✅         | ✅       | ✅     | ✅(仅自己的) | ✅(脱敏) |
| 审核申请       | ✅         | ✅       | ✅     | ❌           | ❌       |
| 推进状态流     | ✅         | ✅       | ✅     | ❌           | ❌       |
| 管理预约       | ✅         | ✅       | ✅     | ✅(仅自己的) | ❌       |
| 退款审批       | ✅         | ✅       | ❌     | ❌           | ❌       |
| 退款操作(财务) | ✅         | ❌       | ❌     | ❌           | ❌       |
| 查看退款记录   | ✅         | ✅       | ✅     | ✅(仅自己的) | ✅(脱敏) |
| 导出数据       | ✅         | ✅       | ❌     | ❌           | ❌       |

### API 接口

```typescript
// 获取申请列表
GET /api/admin/bank-applications
Params: { bankCode?: string; openMode?: 'witness' | 'visit_hk' | 'remote'; status?: BankApplicationStatus; keyword?: string; page?: number; pageSize?: number; }

// 推进状态
POST /api/admin/bank-applications/:id/status-transition
Body: { targetStatus: BankApplicationStatus; notes: string; appointment?: AppointmentInfo; }

// 退款操作
POST /api/admin/bank-applications/:id/refund
Body: { action: 'apply' | 'approve' | 'reject'; amount: number; reason: string; approvalStep?: 'ops' | 'finance' | 'exec'; }
```

---

## 8.5.3 AI知识库管理页

### 页面概览

AI知识库管理页采用经典的 **左侧分类树 + 右侧内容区** 双栏布局。左侧展示多级知识分类与条目统计，右侧展示选中分类下的知识条目卡片，支持增删改查、批量导入、向量检索测试。本页面是AI Agent系统的核心数据源管理入口。

### 完整线框图

```
+==========================================================================================+
| [Logo] 太初国链 Admin                        [🔍] [🔔12] [👤 Admin ▼]    Dark Theme      |
```

### 知识卡片组件规格

```
+===========================================================================================+
|  知识卡片组件 (ProCard)                                                                   |
+===========================================================================================+
|                                                                                           |
|  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ |
|  │ 🔴 顶部状态条 (4px 高度) — 颜色编码                                                  │ |
|  │ ━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━  │ |
|  │ 🟢 绿色=已发布   🟡 黄色=待核验   🔴 红色=已驳回   ⚪ 灰色=草稿                       │ |
|  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ |
|                                                                                           |
|  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ |
|  │                                                                                      │ |
|  │  标题: 中国企业所得税法实施条例第91条 — 跨境所得                                     │ |
|  │  副标题: 适用于非居民企业取得来源于中国境内的所得                                     │ |
|  │                                                                                      │ |
|  │  ┌──────────────┐ ┌──────────────┐ ┌──────────────┐ ┌──────────────┐              │ |
|  │  │ 📊 税率       │ │ 📅 生效日期   │ │ 📋 状态       │ │ 🔗 来源       │              │ |
|  │  │   25%        │ │ 2008-01-01   │ │ ✅ 已发布    │ │ 国税总局      │              │ |
|  │  └──────────────┘ └──────────────┘ └──────────────┘ └──────────────┘              │ |
|  │                                                                                      │ |
|  │  内容摘要:                                                                            │ |
|  │  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │ |
|  │  │ 非居民企业取得企业所得税法第三条第三款规定的所得，按照下列方法计算其应纳税    │   │ |
|  │  │ 所得额：...                                                                   │   │ |
|  │  │ [展开完整内容]                                                                │   │ |
|  │  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │ |
|  │                                                                                      │ |
|  │  元数据:                                                                              │ |
|  │  ┌──────────────┐ ┌──────────────┐ ┌──────────────┐ ┌──────────────┐              │ |
|  │  │ 👤 核验人     │ │ 📅 核验日期   │ │ 🏷️ 标签       │ │ 🆔 条目ID     │              │ |
|  │  │ 王律师       │ │ 2025-01-10   │ │ 跨境,所得税   │ │ K-10091      │              │ |
|  │  └──────────────┘ └──────────────┘ └──────────────┘ └──────────────┘              │ |
|  │                                                                                      │ |
|  │  向量: 已嵌入 (1536维)   相似度阈值: 0.75   最后索引: 2025-01-10 14:32               │ |
|  │                                                                                      │ |
```

### 权限矩阵

| 功能           | 超级管理员 | 知识管理员 | 审核员 | 普通用户 | 访客       |
| -------------- | ---------- | ---------- | ------ | -------- | ---------- |
| 查看知识条目   | ✅         | ✅         | ✅     | ✅       | ✅(已发布) |
| 新增/编辑/删除 | ✅         | ✅         | ❌     | ❌       | ❌         |
| 批量导入/导出  | ✅         | ✅         | ❌     | ❌       | ❌         |
| 向量检索测试   | ✅         | ✅         | ✅     | ❌       | ❌         |
| 核验知识       | ✅         | ✅         | ✅     | ❌       | ❌         |
| 管理分类树     | ✅         | ✅         | ❌     | ❌       | ❌         |

### API 接口

```typescript
// 获取分类树
GET /api/admin/kb/categories → KnowledgeCategory[]

// 获取知识条目列表
GET /api/admin/kb/entries
Params: { categoryId?: string; status?: string; verificationStatus?: string; keyword?: string; page?: number; pageSize?: number; }

// 向量检索测试
POST /api/admin/kb/vector-search
Body: { query: string; topK: number; threshold: number; filterCategory?: string; }
Response: { results: { entry: KnowledgeEntry; similarity: number; }[]; latencyMs: number; }

// 同步向量库
POST /api/admin/kb/sync-vectors
Body: { categoryId?: string; forceRecreate?: boolean; }
```

---

## 8.5.4 税率数据库管理页

### 页面概览

税率数据库管理页是平台财税计算的核心数据源管理模块，支持全球200+国家/地区的税种与税率维护。页面设计围绕 **国家选择器 → 税率编辑器 → 批量导入 → 版本历史** 四大功能区展开，确保税率数据的准确性、可追溯性。每个税率变更都有完整的审计追踪。

### 完整线框图

```
+==========================================================================================+
```

### 数据模型

```typescript
interface TaxRate {
  id: string; // "CN-VAT-STD-2019"
  countryCode: string; // ISO 3166-1 alpha-2
  countryName: string;
  flagEmoji: string;
  taxType: string; // "VAT_STANDARD"
  taxTypeName: string;
  taxRate: number; // 0.13 (表示13%)
  taxRateDisplay: string;
  effectiveDate: string;
  expiryDate?: string;
  sourceUrl: string;
  sourceName: string;
  sourceDocumentNo?: string;
  verificationStatus: 'verified' | 'pending' | 'disputed' | 'outdated';
  verifierId?: string;
  verifierName?: string;
  verifiedAt?: string;
  notes?: string;
  isFavorite: boolean;
  createdAt: string;
  updatedAt: string;
  updatedBy: string;
  version: number;
}

interface TaxRateHistory {
  id: string;
  taxRateId: string;
  version: number;
  changedAt: string;
  changedBy: string;
  changedByName: string;
  oldValue: Partial<TaxRate>;
  newValue: Partial<TaxRate>;
  changeReason: string;
  sourceDocument?: string;
  sourceDocumentUrl?: string;
  isRollback: boolean;
}
```

### 核验状态映射

| 状态      | 徽章         | 背景色    | 文字色    | 含义               | 触发条件            |
| --------- | ------------ | --------- | --------- | ------------------ | ------------------- |
| ✅ 已核验 | `Success`    | `#1B2E1B` | `#5BD46E` | 数据经专业核验确认 | 税务专员确认后标记  |
| 🔄 核验中 | `Processing` | `#1D2B2B` | `#5BD4D0` | 待核验或复核中     | 新增/编辑后自动进入 |
| ⚠️ 有争议 | `Warning`    | `#2B1D11` | `#D46B08` | 多方数据不一致     | 系统检测到冲突      |
| ❌ 已过期 | `Error`      | `#2E1B1B` | `#D45050` | 税率已失效         | 超过失效日期        |

### 权限矩阵

| 功能          | 超级管理员 | 税务专员 | 审核员 | 普通用户   |
| ------------- | ---------- | -------- | ------ | ---------- |
| 查看税率      | ✅         | ✅       | ✅     | ✅(已核验) |
| 新增/编辑税率 | ✅         | ✅       | ❌     | ❌         |
| 批量导入      | ✅         | ✅       | ❌     | ❌         |
| 核验税率      | ✅         | ✅       | ✅     | ❌         |
| 查看版本历史  | ✅         | ✅       | ✅     | ✅(部分)   |
| 回退版本      | ✅         | ✅       | ❌     | ❌         |

### API 接口

```typescript
GET    /api/admin/tax-rates?countryCode=&taxType=&verificationStatus=&page=&pageSize= → TaxRate[]
PATCH  /api/admin/tax-rates/:id → Partial<TaxRate>
POST   /api/admin/tax-rates/import → FormData (file, errorStrategy, overwriteExisting)
GET    /api/admin/tax-rates/:id/history → TaxRateHistory[]
POST   /api/admin/tax-rates/:id/rollback → { targetVersionId, reason }
```

---

## 8.5.5 法规库管理页

### 页面概览

法规库管理页以 **卡片网格** 形式展示全球法规条目，每条法规以卡片呈现核心元数据，点击后弹出详情弹窗。页面支持按国家、行业、法规类型等多维度筛选，并提供新法规邮件通知设置。

### 完整线框图

```
|  │                                                                                      │ |
|  │  • 第38条: 跨境提供个人信息需通过安全评估，可能涉及向境外实体传输数据                 │ |
|  │    → 若接收方位于受制裁国家/地区，需额外进行制裁筛查                                   │ |
|  │    → 建议: 建立数据出境审查流程，将制裁筛查纳入PIPL合规体系                            │ |
|  │                                                                                      │ |
|  │  • 第42条: 境外的组织、个人从事损害中华人民共和国公民的个人信息权益的...               │ |
|  │    → 可能涉及对特定国家/地区服务提供商的限制                                          │ |
|  │    → 建议: 定期审查境外服务商的制裁合规状态                                           │ |
|  │                                                                                      │ |
|  │  相关制裁名单: OFAC (搜索 "数据服务" 类别: 0 条匹配)                                  │ |
|  │                                                                                      │ |
|  │  综合建议: 建立数据出境 → 制裁筛查的联动检查机制，在PIPL合规流程中嵌入制裁检查节点     │ |
```

### 权限矩阵

| 功能          | 超级管理员 | 合规官 | 法务专员 | 普通用户   |
| ------------- | ---------- | ------ | -------- | ---------- |
| 查看法规      | ✅         | ✅     | ✅       | ✅(已发布) |
| 新增/编辑法规 | ✅         | ✅     | ❌       | ❌         |
| 管理合规清单  | ✅         | ✅     | ✅       | ❌         |
| 配置通知      | ✅         | ✅     | ✅       | ✅(个人)   |
| 查看制裁风险  | ✅         | ✅     | ✅       | ✅(摘要)   |
| 导出法规      | ✅         | ✅     | ✅       | ❌         |

### API 接口

```typescript
GET  /api/admin/regulations?countryCodes=&industries=&categories=&status=&sanctionRiskLevel=&keyword=&page=&pageSize= → Regulation[]
GET  /api/admin/regulations/:id → Regulation
POST /api/admin/regulations/:id/checklist → { itemId, isCompleted }
PUT  /api/admin/regulations/notification-settings → RegulationNotification
```

---

## 8.5.6 合同模板管理页

### 页面概览

合同模板管理页是法务运营中心的核心工具，支持按业务场景分类管理标准化合同模板。页面采用 **场景标签 → 模板卡片网格 → 模板编辑器** 三层架构，模板编辑器采用左右分栏设计（左侧变量列表 + 右侧实时渲染预览），支持下载 Word/PDF 和变量自定义。

### 完整线框图

```
+==========================================================================================+
| [Logo] 太初国链 Admin                        [🔍] [🔔12] [👤 Admin ▼]    Dark Theme      |
+==========================================================================================+
| [Sidebar]      |                                                                         |
|                |  Breadcrumb: 首页 / 合规管理 / 合同模板                                   |
|                |                                                                         |
|                |  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ |

|                |  │                                                                      │ |
|                |  │ [🛒 B2C电商    14] [🏭 B2B批发     8] [💻 SaaS订阅   10]         │ |
|                |  │ [🚚 物流服务     6] [👔 雇佣合同     5] [🏠 房屋租赁     3]         │ |
|                |  │ [🤝 合作协议     7] [🔒 保密协议     9] [📋 全部        62]         │ |
```

```
|  │  67    {{company_name}}的联系方式如下...                                              │ |

|                                                                                          |
|                        [取消]  [🗑️ 删除变量]  [💾 保存]                                  |
+==========================================================================================+
```

### 数据模型

```typescript
type ContractScenario =
  | 'b2c'
  | 'b2b'
  | 'saas'
  | 'logistics'
  | 'employment'
  | 'housing'
  | 'cooperation'
  | 'nda';

interface ContractTemplate {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  nameEn: string;
  scenario: ContractScenario;
  scenarioLabel: string;
  version: string;
  status: 'draft' | 'reviewing' | 'published' | 'deprecated';
  languages: string[];
  variableCount: number;
  variables: TemplateVariable[];
  content: string; // Markdown 源码
  contentHtml: string;
  usageCount: number;
  lastUsedAt?: string;
  createdAt: string;
  updatedAt: string;
  createdBy: string;
  updatedBy: string;
  relatedRegulations?: string[];
}

type VariableType =
  | 'text'
  | 'number'
  | 'date'
  | 'select'
  | 'boolean'
  | 'richtext'
  | 'currency'
  | 'percentage';

interface TemplateVariable {
  name: string;
  displayName: string;
  description: string;
  type: VariableType;
  required: boolean;
  defaultValue?: string;
  placeholder?: string;
  maxLength?: number;
  validationRegex?: string;
  validationMessage?: string;
  formatOptions?: {
    trim: boolean;
    capitalize: 'none' | 'first' | 'all' | 'words';
    prefix?: string;
    suffix?: string;
  };
  options?: { label: string; value: string }[];
  conditional?: {
    dependsOn: string;
    operator: 'equals' | 'notEquals' | 'contains' | 'isEmpty';
    value: string;
  };
  multilingual: Record<string, string>;
}
```

### 权限矩阵

| 功能          | 超级管理员 | 法务主管 | 模板编辑 | 普通用户   |
| ------------- | ---------- | -------- | -------- | ---------- |
| 查看模板      | ✅         | ✅       | ✅       | ✅(已发布) |
| 编辑模板      | ✅         | ✅       | ✅       | ❌         |
| 编辑变量      | ✅         | ✅       | ✅       | ❌         |
| 下载Word/PDF  | ✅         | ✅       | ✅       | ✅(已发布) |
| 复制模板      | ✅         | ✅       | ✅       | ❌         |
| 发布/弃用模板 | ✅         | ✅       | ❌       | ❌         |

### API 接口

```typescript
GET  /api/admin/contract-templates?scenario=&status=&language=&keyword=&page=&pageSize= → ContractTemplate[]
PUT  /api/admin/contract-templates/:id → { content, variables, versionNote }
POST /api/admin/contract-templates/:id/preview → { variableValues, language } → { html }
POST /api/admin/contract-templates/:id/download → { format, variableValues } → Blob
```

---

## 8.5.7 DLC等级配置页

### 页面概览

DLC（Decentralized Level Certificate）等级配置页是平台经济系统的核心参数面板，负责定义L1-L9共9个等级的全部配置参数。页面采用 **横向标签切换等级 → 纵向配置面板** 的布局，每个等级包含等级标识、升级条件、特权开关和权重系数四大配置区块。L9为预留荣誉等级，需完成特殊成就方可解锁。

### 完整线框图

```
+==========================================================================================+
| [Logo] 太初国链 Admin                        [🔍] [🔔12] [👤 Admin ▼]    Dark Theme      |
+==========================================================================================+
| [Sidebar]      |                                                                         |
|                |  Breadcrumb: 首页 / DLC管理 / 等级配置                                    |
|                |                                                                         |
|                |  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ |
|                |  │ 等级标签切换栏                                                       │ |
|                |  │                                                                      │ |
|                |  │ [🥉 L1 青铜] [🥉 L2 白银] [🥈 L3 黄金] [🥈 L4 铂金]             │ |
|                |  │ [🥇 L5 钻石] [💎 L6 星耀] [💎 L7 王者] [👑 L8 传奇]             │ |
|                |  │ [👑 L9 神话 (预留)]                                                 │ |
|                |  │                                                                      │ |
|                |  │ 当前编辑: 🥈 L3 黄金    用户数: 1,250    状态: ✅ 启用             │ |
|                |  │                                                                      │ |
|                |  │ [📊 查看总览]  [🔄 重置当前等级]  [📋 复制到其他等级]               │ |
|                |  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ |
|                |                                                                         |
|                |  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ |
|                |  │ 等级基本信息                                                         │ |
|                |  │                                                                      │ |
|                |  │  等级名称:     [🥈 L3 黄金             ]    (显示名称)              │ |
|                |  │  英文名:       [Gold Member             ]                              │ |
|                |  │  等级图标:     [🥈 ▼]  (从图标库选择，支持上传自定义)                │ |
|                |  │  主题颜色:     [■ #FFD700 ▼]  预览: ████████████  文字色: [自动计算] │ |
|                |  │  等级描述:     [黄金会员享有优先分发渠道和更高的...           ]       │ |
|                |  │  等级徽章:     [👁 预览徽章]  (用于在用户资料页展示)                   │ |
|                |  │  是否启用:     ☑️ 是                                                  │ |
|                |  │  显示顺序:     [3        ]  (1-9，影响展示排序)                       │ |
|                |  │  是否为荣誉等级: ☐ 否    (荣誉等级不参与常规升级)                      │ |
|                |  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ |
|                |                                                                         |
|                |  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ |
|                |  │ 升级条件                                                            │ |
|                |  │                                                                      │ |
|                |  │  条件类型          运算符    阈值          单位     是否必须  权重   │ |
|                |  │  ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────     │ |
|                |  │  DVC余额          >=      [1000      ]  DVC      ☑️       1.0    │ |
|                |  │  累计交易金额      >=      [50000     ]  USD      ☑️       1.0    │ |
|                |  │  内容发布数        >=      [50       ]  篇        ☐       0.5    │ |
|                |  │  粉丝数           >=      [1000      ]  人        ☐       0.5    │ |
|                |  │  连续活跃天数      >=      [30       ]  天        ☑️       1.0    │ |
|                |  │  邀请用户数        >=      [10       ]  人        ☐       0.3    │ |
|                |  │  质押DVC数量       >=      [500      ]  DVC      ☐       0.7    │ |
|                |  │  社区贡献值        >=      [100      ]  分        ☐       0.5    │ |
|                |  │                                                                      │ |
|                |  │  [+ 添加条件]    条件逻辑: [全部满足 ▼] / [满足任意] / [加权评分]    │ |

|                |  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ |
|                |                                                                         |

|                |  │  🛡️ 内容保护等级            ☑️ ON   [水印+指纹 ▼]    防盗版保护级别     │ |

|                |  │                                                                      │ |

|                |                                                                         |
```
